Component Module Structure\n```\ncomponents/camel-fix/\n├── pom.xml\n└── src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/\n    ├── FixComponent.java\n    ├── FixEndpoint.java\n    ├── FixProducer.java\n    ├── FixConsumer.java\n    ├── FixConfiguration.java\n    └── FixConstants.java\n```\n\n## Files to Modify\n\n### 1. `/workspace/components/pom.xml`\n- Add `<module>camel-fix</module>` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### Phase 1: Define Types and Configuration\n1. **FixConstants.java** - Header constants for FIX message metadata\n2. **FixConfiguration.java** - POJO with @UriParams for configuration properties\n\n### Phase 2: Core Component Implementation\n3. **FixComponent.java** - Extends DefaultComponent, manages FIX engine lifecycle\n4. **FixEndpoint.java** - Extends DefaultEndpoint, creates Consumer/Producer instances\n\n### Phase 3: Consumer/Producer Implementation\n5. **FixConsumer.java** - Extends DefaultConsumer, receives inbound FIX messages\n6. **FixProducer.java** - Extends DefaultAsyncProducer, sends outbound FIX messages\n\n### Phase 4: Build Integration\n7. **pom.xml** for camel-fix module\n8. Modify components/pom.xml to register the module\n\n## Implementation Patterns\n\n### Component Pattern (from KafkaComponent/SedaComponent)\n- Annotate with `@Component(\"fix\")`\n- Extend `DefaultComponent` or `HealthCheckComponent`\n- Implement `createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters)`\n- Manage configuration via a Configuration POJO\n- Handle lifecycle via `doInit()`/`doShutdown()` methods\n\n### Endpoint Pattern (from KafkaEndpoint)\n- Annotate with `@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\", ...)`\n- Extend `DefaultEndpoint`\n- Implement `createConsumer(Processor processor)` and `createProducer()`\n- Manage configuration properties via `@UriParam` annotations\n\n### Producer Pattern (from KafkaProducer)\n- Extend `DefaultAsyncProducer`\n- Implement `process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback)` for async processing\n- Extract FIX message data from Exchange body/headers\n- Return false on success, true on error to async callback\n\n### Consumer Pattern (from KafkaConsumer)\n- Extend `DefaultConsumer`\n- Implement `doStart()` to initialize FIX session listener\n- Implement `doStop()` to cleanup FIX session\n- Create Exchanges from inbound FIX messages using `createExchange()` and `getProcessor().process()`\n\n### Configuration Pattern\n- POJO with `@UriParam` fields\n- Getter/setter methods for each property\n- Properties: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort\n\n### Constants Pattern (from KafkaConstants)\n- `public static final String` declarations with `@Metadata` annotations\n- Header keys for: FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, FIX_SESSION_ID, FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, etc.\n\n## Code Structure Details\n\n### FixComponent\n```java\n@Component(\"fix\")\npublic class FixComponent extends HealthCheckComponent {\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    protected FixEndpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) {\n        FixEndpoint endpoint = new FixEndpoint(uri, this);\n        endpoint.setConfiguration(getConfiguration().copy());\n        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);\n        return endpoint;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixEndpoint\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\",\n             title = \"FIX\", category = { Category.MESSAGING })\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriParam\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) {\n        FixConsumer consumer = new FixConsumer(this, processor);\n        configureConsumer(consumer);\n        return consumer;\n    }\n\n    public Producer createProducer() {\n        return new FixProducer(this);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixProducer\n```java\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        // Extract FIX message from exchange\n        // Send via FIX session\n        // Call callback.done(true/false)\n        return false; // continue processing sync or async\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixConsumer\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer implements FixSessionListener {\n\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        // Initialize FIX acceptor/initiator\n        // Register this as message listener\n    }\n\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        // Stop FIX session\n    }\n\n    public void onFixMessage(FixMessage msg) {\n        // Create Exchange from FIX message\n        // Process via route\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## URI Format\n- `fix:sessionID?options`\n- Example: `fix:BROKER1?configFile=/etc/fix.cfg&senderCompID=SENDER`\n\n## Key Implementation Points\n\n1. **FIX Protocol Integration**: The component will work with a FIX library (assumed to be available as dependency)\n2. **Session Management**: Component manages FIX acceptor sessions for consumers and initiator for producers\n3. **Message Mapping**: FIX messages are mapped to Camel Exchanges with:\n   - Body: FIX message as serialized bytes or parsed object\n   - Headers: FIX header fields mapped to standard constants\n4. **Configuration**: All FIX properties configurable via URI parameters or component-level settings\n5. **Lifecycle**: Proper initialization/shutdown of FIX engine and sessions\n\n## Testing Considerations\n- Will need FIX test infrastructure (similar to camel-test-infra-kafka)\n- Unit tests for component creation, endpoint creation\n- Integration tests for message sending/receiving\n- Mock FIX session for testing without real broker\n\n## Service Loader Files\nAuto-generated by Camel build tools in:\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-component`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-endpoint`\n\nThese are generated from annotations and should NOT be manually created.\n\n## POM Dependencies\n\n### Build Dependencies\n- `camel-support` - Core Camel support classes\n- `camel-health` - For HealthCheckComponent\n\n### Runtime Dependencies (placeholder for actual FIX library)\n- FIX protocol library (e.g., QuickFIXj or similar)\n- Any FIX library dependencies\n\n### Test Dependencies\n- `camel-test-junit5`\n- `junit-jupiter`\n- `mockito-junit-jupiter`\n\n## Next Steps After Initial Implementation\n\n1. Choose FIX library (QuickFIXj recommended for Java)\n2. Add dependency to pom.xml\n3. Implement actual FIX session handling in Consumer/Producer\n4. Add comprehensive test suite\n5. Add documentation and examples\n6. KafkaProducer)\n- Extend `DefaultAsyncProducer`\n- Implement `process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback)` for async processing\n- Extract FIX message data from Exchange body/headers\n- Return false on success, true on error to async callback\n\n### Consumer Pattern (from KafkaConsumer)\n- Extend `DefaultConsumer`\n- Implement `doStart()` to initialize FIX session listener\n- Implement `doStop()` to cleanup FIX session\n- Create Exchanges from inbound FIX messages using `createExchange()` and `getProcessor().process()`\n\n### Configuration Pattern\n- POJO with `@UriParam` fields\n- Getter/setter methods for each property\n- Properties: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort\n\n### Constants Pattern (from KafkaConstants)\n- `public static final String` declarations with `@Metadata` annotations\n- Header keys for: FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, FIX_SESSION_ID, FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, etc.\n\n## Code Structure Details\n\n### FixComponent\n```java\n@Component(\"fix\")\npublic class FixComponent extends HealthCheckComponent {\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    protected FixEndpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) {\n        FixEndpoint endpoint = new FixEndpoint(uri, this);\n        endpoint.setConfiguration(getConfiguration().copy());\n        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);\n        return endpoint;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixEndpoint\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\",\n             title = \"FIX\", category = { Category.MESSAGING })\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriParam\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) {\n        FixConsumer consumer = new FixConsumer(this, processor);\n        configureConsumer(consumer);\n        return consumer;\n    }\n\n    public Producer createProducer() {\n        return new FixProducer(this);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixProducer\n```java\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        // Extract FIX message from exchange\n        // Send via FIX session\n        // Call callback.done(true/false)\n        return false; // continue processing sync or async\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixConsumer\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer implements FixSessionListener {\n\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        // Initialize FIX acceptor/initiator\n        // Register this as message listener\n    }\n\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        // Stop FIX session\n    }\n\n    public void onFixMessage(FixMessage msg) {\n        // Create Exchange from FIX message\n        // Process via route\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## URI Format\n- `fix:sessionID?options`\n- Example: `fix:BROKER1?configFile=/etc/fix.cfg&senderCompID=SENDER`\n\n## Key Implementation Points\n\n1. **FIX Protocol Integration**: The component will work with a FIX library (assumed to be available as dependency)\n2. **Session Management**: Component manages FIX acceptor sessions for consumers and initiator for producers\n3. **Message Mapping**: FIX messages are mapped to Camel Exchanges with:\n   - Body: FIX message as serialized bytes or parsed object\n   - Headers: FIX header fields mapped to standard constants\n4. **Configuration**: All FIX properties configurable via URI parameters or component-level settings\n5. **Lifecycle**: Proper initialization/shutdown of FIX engine and sessions\n\n## Testing Considerations\n- Will need FIX test infrastructure (similar to camel-test-infra-kafka)\n- Unit tests for component creation, endpoint creation\n- Integration tests for message sending/receiving\n- Mock FIX session for testing without real broker\n\n## Service Loader Files\nAuto-generated by Camel build tools in:\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-component`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-endpoint`\n\nThese are generated from annotations and should NOT be manually created.\n\n## POM Dependencies\n\n### Build Dependencies\n- `camel-support` - Core Camel support classes\n- `camel-health` - For HealthCheckComponent\n\n### Runtime Dependencies (placeholder for actual FIX library)\n- FIX protocol library (e.g., QuickFIXj or similar)\n- Any FIX library dependencies\n\n### Test Dependencies\n- `camel-test-junit5`\n- `junit-jupiter`\n- `mockito-junit-jupiter`\n\n## Next Steps After Initial Implementation\n\n1. Choose FIX library (QuickFIXj recommended for Java)\n2. Add dependency to pom.xml\n3. Implement actual FIX session handling in Consumer/Producer\n4. Add comprehensive test suite\n5. 58→    public SedaConsumer(SedaEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n    59→        super(endpoint, processor);\n    60→        this.pollTimeout = endpoint.getPollTimeout();\n    61→    }\n    62→\n    63→    @Override\n    64→    public SedaEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n    65→        return (SedaEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    66→    }\n    67→\n    68→    @Override\n    69→    public boolean deferShutdown(ShutdownRunningTask shutdownRunningTask) {\n    70→        // deny stopping on shutdown as we want seda consumers to run in case some other queues\n    71→        // depend on this consumer to run, so it can complete its exchanges\n    72→        return true;\n    73→    }\n    74→\n    75→    @Override\n    76→    public int getPendingExchangesSize() {\n    77→        // the route is shutting down, so either we should purge the queue,\n    78→        // or return how many exchanges are still on the queue\n    79→        if (getEndpoint().isPurgeWhenStopping()) {\n    80→            getEndpoint().purgeQueue();\n    81→        }\n    82→        return getEndpoint().getQueue().size();\n    83→    }\n    84→\n    85→    @Override\n    86→    public void prepareShutdown(boolean suspendOnly, boolean forced) {\n    87→        // if we are suspending then we want to keep the thread running but just not route the exchange\n    88→        // this logic is only when we stop or shutdown the consumer\n    89→        if (suspendOnly) {\n    90→            LOG.debug(\"Skip preparing to shutdown as consumer is being suspended\");\n    91→            return;\n    92→        }\n    93→\n    94→        // signal we want to shutdown\n    95→        shutdownPending = true;\n    96→        forceShutdown = forced;\n    97→\n    98→        if (latch != null) {\n    99→            LOG.debug(\"Preparing to shutdown, waiting for {} consumer threads to complete.\", latch.getCount());\n   100→\n   101→            // wait for all threads to end\n   102→            try {\n   103→                latch.await();\n   104→            } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n   105→                Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n   106→            }\n   107→        }\n   108→    }\n   109→\n   110→    @Override\n   111→    public boolean isRunAllowed() {\n   112→        // if we force shutdown then do not allow running anymore\n   113→        if LOG.debug(\"Skip preparing to shutdown as consumer is being suspended\");\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // signal we want to shutdown\n        shutdownPending = true;\n        forceShutdown = forced;\n\n        if (latch != null) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Preparing to shutdown, waiting for {} consumer threads to complete.\", latch.getCount());\n\n            // wait for all threads to end\n            try {\n                latch.await();\n            } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n            }\n        }\n org.apache.camel.Category;\nimport org.apache.camel.Consumer;\nimport org.apache.camel.Processor;\nimport org.apache.camel.Producer;\nimport org.apache.camel.spi.EndpointServiceLocation;\nimport FixConstants.class)\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint implements EndpointServiceLocation {\n\n    @UriParam(label = \"common\")\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    public FixEndpoint() {\n    }\n\n    public FixEndpoint(String endpointUri, FixComponent component) {\n        super(endpointUri, component);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixComponent getComponent() {\n        return (FixComponent) super.getComponent();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) throws Exception {\n        FixConsumer consumer = new FixConsumer(this, processor);\n        configureConsumer(consumer);\n        return consumer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Producer createProducer() throws Exception org.apache.camel.AsyncCallback;\nimport org.apache.camel.Exchange;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.DefaultAsyncProducer;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\n\n/**\n * A producer for sending FIX messages\n */\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixProducer.class);\n\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n    private final FixConfiguration configuration;\n\n    public FixProducer(FixEndpoint endpoint) {\n        super(endpoint);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n        this.configuration = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        try {\n            Object body = exchange.getIn().getBody();\n\n            if (body == null) {\n                exchange.setException(new IllegalArgumentException(\"FIX message body cannot be null\"));\n                callback.done(false);\n                return false;\n            }\n\n            // TODO: Send the FIX message via the FIX session\n            LOG.debug(\"Sending FIX message: {}\", body);\n\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, \"OUTBOUND\");\n\n            callback.done(false);\n            return false;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.error(\"Error sending FIX message\", e);\n            exchange.setException(e);\n            callback.done(false);\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n        // TODO: Initialize FIX initiator connection\n        LOG.debug(\"Starting FixProducer with configuration: {}\", configuration);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        // TODO: Cleanup FIX initiator connection\n        LOG.debug(\"Stopping FixProducer\");\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 7. `/workspace/components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java`\n\n```java\npackage org.apache.camel.component.fix;\n\nimport org.apache.camel.Exchange;\nimport org.apache.camel.Processor;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.DefaultConsumer;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\n\n/**\n * A consumer for receiving FIX messages\n */\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n    private final FixConfiguration configuration;\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n        this.endpoint = endpoint;\n        this.configuration = endpoint.getConfiguration();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n        // TODO: Initialize FIX acceptor session\n        LOG.debug(\"Starting FixConsumer with configuration: {}\", configuration);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        // TODO: Cleanup FIX acceptor session\n        LOG.debug(\"Stopping FixConsumer\");\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Process an incoming FIX message\n     */\n    public void onFixMessage(String message) {\n        try {\n            Exchange exchange = createExchange(false);\n            exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, \"INBOUND\");\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, endpoint.getEndpointUri());\n\n            // Process the exchange through the route\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.error(\"Error processing FIX message\", e);\n            getExceptionHandler().handleException(e);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 8. `/workspace/components/pom.xml` - Registration\n\n```diff\nIndex: components/pom.xml\n--- a/components/pom.xml\n+++ b/components/pom.xml\n@@ -138,6 +138,7 @@\n message processing\n- Handles lifecycle with `doStart()` and `doStop()`\n- Proper exception handling and logging\n\n**Consumer Pattern** ✓\n- Extends `DefaultConsumer`\n- Implements message processing callback `onFixMessage()`\n- Uses `createExchange(boolean)` with correct signature\n- Proper lifecycle management (doStart/doStop)\n- Uses `getProcessor()` to route messages through Camel\n\n**Configuration Pattern** ✓\n- POJO with `@UriParams` class annotation\n- All configuration properties have `@UriParam` annotations\n- Properties: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort\n- Includes copy constructor for proper configuration duplication\n\n**Constants Pattern** ✓\n- All header constants use `public static final String`\n- Each constant has `@Metadata` annotation with description and javaType\n- Headers: FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, FIX_SESSION_ID, FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, Pattern Adherence\n\n**Component Pattern** ✓\n- Extends `HealthCheckComponent` (extends DefaultComponent)\n- Annotated with `@Component(\"fix\")`\n- Implements `createEndpoint()` to create FIX endpoints\n- Manages shared configuration via FixConfiguration POJO\n- Properly delegates configuration properties\n\n**Endpoint Pattern** ✓\n- Extends `DefaultEndpoint`\n- Implements `EndpointServiceLocation` interface for service discovery\n- Annotated with `@UriEndpoint` with proper metadata\n- URI format: `fix:sessionID?options`\n- Implements `createConsumer()` and `createProducer()`\n- Configuration properties with `@UriParam` annotations\n\n**Producer Pattern** ✓\n- Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`\n- Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` for async message processing\n- Handles lifecycle with `doStart()` and `doStop()`\n- Proper exception handling and logging\n\n**Consumer Pattern** ✓\n- Extends `DefaultConsumer`\n- Implements message processing callback `onFixMessage()`\n- Uses `createExchange(boolean)` with correct signature\n- Proper lifecycle management (doStart/doStop)\n- Uses `getProcessor()` to route messages through Camel\n\n**Configuration Pattern** ✓\n- POJO with `@UriParams` class annotation\n- All configuration properties have `@UriParam` annotations\n- Properties: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort\n- Includes copy constructor for proper configuration duplication\n\n**Constants Pattern** ✓\n- All header constants use `public static final String`\n- Each constant has `@Metadata` annotation with description and javaType\n- Headers: FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, FIX_SESSION_ID, FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, FIX_SEQUENCE_NUMBER, FIX_TIMESTAMP\n\n### Build Integration\n\n1. **Module Registration**: camel-fix is correctly added to components/pom.xml in alphabetical order\n2. **POM Inheritance**: Component POM correctly inherits from components parent\n3. **Dependency Management**: Dependencies properly declared (camel-support, camel-health)\n4. **Service Loader**: Auto-generated by Camel build tools in the `generated` folder\n\n### Compilation Status\n\n✅ **BUILD SUCCESS** - All classes compile without errors\n- No syntax errors\n- All type signatures correct\n- All necessary imports included\n- Proper interface implementations\n\n---\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **HealthCheckComponent**: Chosen over DefaultComponent to support health checks for FIX sessions\n2. **EndpointServiceLocation**: Implemented to support service discovery and monitoring\n3. **DefaultAsyncProducer**: Used to support async message sending\n4. **Copy Constructor**: Configuration includes copy() method for proper endpoint-level configuration isolation\n5. **Placeholder Implementation**: Producer and Consumer include TODO comments for actual FIX library integration\n\n---\n\n## Apache Camel FIX Component Implementation Plan\n\n## Objective\nImplement a new `camel-fix` component for Apache Camel that enables routing FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol messages through Camel routes.\n\n## Files to Create\n\n### 1. Component Module Structure\n```\ncomponents/camel-fix/\n├── pom.xml\n└── src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/\n    ├── FixComponent.java\n    ├── FixEndpoint.java\n    ├── FixProducer.java\n    ├── FixConsumer.java\n    ├── FixConfiguration.java\n    └── FixConstants.java\n```\n\n## Files to Modify\n\n### 1. `/workspace/components/pom.xml`\n- Add `<module>camel-fix</module>` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### Phase 1: Define Types and Configuration\n1. **FixConstants.java** - Header constants for FIX message metadata\n2. **FixConfiguration.java** - POJO with @UriParams for configuration properties\n\n### Phase 2: Core Component Implementation\n3. **FixComponent.java** - Extends DefaultComponent, manages FIX engine lifecycle\n4. **FixEndpoint.java** - Extends DefaultEndpoint, creates Consumer/Producer instances\n\n### Phase 3: Consumer/Producer Implementation\n5. **FixConsumer.java** - Extends DefaultConsumer, receives inbound FIX messages\n6. **FixProducer.java** - Extends DefaultAsyncProducer, sends outbound FIX messages\n\n### Phase 4: Build Integration\n7. **pom.xml** for camel-fix module\n8. Modify components/pom.xml to register the module\n\n## Implementation Patterns\n\n### Component Pattern (from KafkaComponent/SedaComponent)\n- Annotate with `@Component(\"fix\")`\n- Extend `DefaultComponent` or `HealthCheckComponent`\n- Implement `createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters)`\n- Manage configuration via a Configuration POJO\n- Handle lifecycle via `doInit()`/`doShutdown()` methods\n\n### Endpoint Pattern (from KafkaEndpoint)\n- Annotate with `@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\", ...)`\n- Extend `DefaultEndpoint`\n- Implement `createConsumer(Processor processor)` and `createProducer()`\n- Manage configuration properties via `@UriParam` annotations\n\n### Producer Pattern (from KafkaProducer)\n- Extend `DefaultAsyncProducer`\n- Implement `process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback)` for async processing\n- Extract FIX message data from Exchange body/headers\n- Return false on success, true on error to async callback\n\n### Consumer Pattern (from KafkaConsumer)\n- Extend `DefaultConsumer`\n- Implement `doStart()` to initialize FIX session listener\n- Implement `doStop()` to cleanup FIX session\n- Create Exchanges from inbound FIX messages using `createExchange()` and `getProcessor().process()`\n\n### Configuration Pattern\n- POJO with `@UriParam` fields\n- Getter/setter methods for each property\n- Properties: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort\n\n### Constants Pattern (from KafkaConstants)\n- `public static final String` declarations with `@Metadata` annotations\n- Header keys for: FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, FIX_SESSION_ID, FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, etc.\n\n## Code Structure Details\n\n### FixComponent\n```java\n@Component(\"fix\")\npublic class FixComponent extends HealthCheckComponent {\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    protected FixEndpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) {\n        FixEndpoint endpoint = new FixEndpoint(uri, this);\n        endpoint.setConfiguration(getConfiguration().copy());\n        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);\n        return endpoint;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixEndpoint\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\",\n             title = \"FIX\", category = { Category.MESSAGING })\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriParam\n    private FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n\n    public Consumer createConsumer(Processor processor) {\n        FixConsumer consumer = new FixConsumer(this, processor);\n        configureConsumer(consumer);\n        return consumer;\n    }\n\n    public Producer createProducer() {\n        return new FixProducer(this);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixProducer\n```java\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        // Extract FIX message from exchange\n        // Send via FIX session\n        // Call callback.done(true/false)\n        return false; // continue processing sync or async\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FixConsumer\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer implements FixSessionListener {\n\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        // Initialize FIX acceptor/initiator\n        // Register this as message listener\n    }\n\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        // Stop FIX session\n    }\n\n    public void onFixMessage(FixMessage msg) {\n        // Create Exchange from FIX message\n        // Process via route\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## URI Format\n- `fix:sessionID?options`\n- Example: `fix:BROKER1?configFile=/etc/fix.cfg&senderCompID=SENDER`\n\n## Key Implementation Points\n\n1. **FIX Protocol Integration**: The component will work with a FIX library (assumed to be available as dependency)\n2. **Session Management**: Component manages FIX acceptor sessions for consumers and initiator for producers\n3. **Message Mapping**: FIX messages are mapped to Camel Exchanges with:\n   - Body: FIX message as serialized bytes or parsed object\n   - Headers: FIX header fields mapped to standard constants\n4. **Configuration**: All FIX properties configurable via URI parameters or component-level settings\n5. **Lifecycle**: Proper initialization/shutdown of FIX engine and sessions\n\n## Testing Considerations\n- Will need FIX test infrastructure (similar to camel-test-infra-kafka)\n- Unit tests for component creation, endpoint creation\n- Integration tests for message sending/receiving\n- Mock FIX session for testing without real broker\n\n## Service Loader Files\nAuto-generated by Camel build tools in:\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-component`\n- `src/generated/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/configurer/fix-endpoint`\n\nThese are generated from annotations and should NOT be manually created.\n\n## POM Dependencies\n\n### Build Dependencies\n- `camel-support` - Core Camel support classes\n- `camel-health` - For
